# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements
This is cross product, not a times symbol ^wIawfHys

Consider the right hand screw rule.  ^pCcTKX8i

Remember that like with matrix multiplication, AxB does not equal B x A. Therefore we cannot factorize a out. ^ajR4ICLX

Because if they were parallel we could get a cross product of 0 ^l3REqQ5d
